var(--shiki-color-text)\">);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p><i id=\"p_47\" class=\"pid\"></i>An expression, <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">E</span></span>, in a statement position is equivalent to the block statement <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">{ </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_return\" title=\"rsh: return\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">return</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">E</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">; }</span></span>.<a href=\"#p_47\" class=\"pid\">47</a></p>\n<h2 id=\"ref-programs-compute-exprs\" class=\"refHeader\">Expressions<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#ref-programs-compute-exprs\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h2>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_48\" class=\"pid\"></i>This section describes the expressions which are allowed in any Reach context.\n  There are a large variety of different <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_expressions\">expressions</span> in Reach programs.<a href=\"#p_48\" class=\"pid\">48</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_49\" class=\"pid\"></i>The remainder of this section enumerates each kind of expression.<a href=\"#p_49\" class=\"pid\">49</a></p>\n<h3 id=\"unstrict\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>unstrict</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#unstrict\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_unstrict\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"unstrict\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"assert(unstrict(() => {\n  'use strict';\n  // the following fails in strict mode due to a type mismatch\n  return 1 != true;\n}));\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn23\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_assert\" title=\"rsh: assert\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">assert</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_unstrict\" title=\"rsh: unstrict\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">unstrict</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(() </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_=%3E\" title=\"rsh: =>\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=&gt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> {</span></li><li value=\"2\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">  </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_'use%20strict'\" title=\"rsh: 'use strict'\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'use strict'</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">;</span></li><li value=\"3\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">  </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// the following fails in strict mode due to a type mismatch</span></li><li value=\"4\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">  </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_return\" title=\"rsh: return\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">return</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">1</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_!=\" title=\"rsh: !=\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">!=</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">;</span></li><li value=\"5\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">}));</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_50\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_unstrict\" title=\"rsh: unstrict\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">unstrict</span></a></span> applies a thunk, ignoring any usage of strict mode. This\n  can be useful when dealing with libraries that are written in strict mode.<a href=\"#p_50\" class=\"pid\">50</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"identifier-reference\" class=\"refHeader\">Identifier reference<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#identifier-reference\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"X\nY\nZ\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn24\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">X</span></li><li value=\"2\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Y</span></li><li value=\"3\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Z</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p><i id=\"p_51\" class=\"pid\"></i>An identifier, written <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">ID</span></span>, is an expression that evaluates to the value of the bound identifier.<a href=\"#p_51\" class=\"pid\">51</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_52\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_this\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"this\"></span>The identifier <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_this\" title=\"rsh: this\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">this</span></a></span> has a special meaning inside of a local step (i.e. the body of an <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/step/#rsh_only\" title=\"rsh: only\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">only</span></a></span> or <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/step/#rsh_each\" title=\"rsh: each\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">each</span></a></span> expression), as well as in a consensus step (i.e. the tail of <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/step/#rsh_publish\" title=\"rsh: publish\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">publish</span></a></span> or <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/step/#rsh_pay\" title=\"rsh: pay\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">pay</span></a></span> statement and before a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_commit\" title=\"rsh: commit\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">commit</span></a></span> statement). For details, see <a href=\"/rsh/local/#ref-programs-local-this\">this</a> and <a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#ref-programs-consensus-this\">this</a>.<a href=\"#p_52\" class=\"pid\">52</a></p>\n<h3 id=\"function-application\" class=\"refHeader\">Function application<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#function-application\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"assert( amount <= heap1 )\nstep( moveA )\ndigest( coinFlip )\ninteract.random()\ndeclassify( _coinFlip )\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn25\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_assert\" title=\"rsh: assert\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">assert</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">( amount </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%3C=\" title=\"rsh: <=\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&lt;=</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> heap1 )</span></li><li value=\"2\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">step</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">( moveA )</span></li><li value=\"3\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_digest\" title=\"rsh: digest\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">digest</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">( coinFlip )</span></li><li value=\"4\"><a href=\"/rsh/local/#rsh_interact\" title=\"rsh: interact\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">interact</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.random</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">()</span></li><li value=\"5\"><a href=\"/rsh/local/#rsh_declassify\" title=\"rsh: declassify\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">declassify</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">( _coinFlip )</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_53\" class=\"pid\"></i>A <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_function%20application\">function application</span>, written <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">EXPR_rator</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(EXPR_rand_0</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">...</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> EXPR_rand_n)</span></span>, is an expression where <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">EXPR_rator</span></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">EXPR_rand_0</span></span> through <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">EXPR_rand_n</span></span> are expressions that evaluate to one value.\n  <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">EXPR_rator</span></span> must evaluate to an abstraction over <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">n</span></span> values or a primitive of arity <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">n</span></span>.\n  A spread expression (<span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">...</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">expr</span></span>) may appear in the list of operands to a function application, in which case the elements of the expr are spliced in place.\n  <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">EXPR_rator</span></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">EXPR_rand_n</span></span> are evaluated in left-to-right order, starting with <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">EXPR_rator</span></span>, then <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">EXPR_rand_0</span></span>, <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">EXPR_rand_1</span></span>, etc.<a href=\"#p_53\" class=\"pid\">53</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_54\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_new\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"new\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Map.new\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Map.new\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Set.new\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Set.new\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Token.new\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Token.new\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_new\" title=\"rsh: new\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">new</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">f</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(a)</span></span> is equivalent to <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">f</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_new\" title=\"rsh: new\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.new</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(a)</span></span> and is a convenient short-hand for writing class-oriented programs.<a href=\"#p_54\" class=\"pid\">54</a></p>\n<h3 id=\"ref-programs-types\" class=\"refHeader\">Types<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#ref-programs-types\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><i id=\"p_55\" class=\"pid\"></i>Reach's <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_type\">type</span>s are represented in programs by the following identifiers and constructors:<a href=\"#p_55\" class=\"pid\">55</a></p>\n<ul>\n  <li><i id=\"p_56\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Null\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Null\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Null\" title=\"rsh: Null\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Null</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_56\" class=\"pid\">56</a></li>\n  <li><i id=\"p_57\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Bool\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Bool\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Bool\" title=\"rsh: Bool\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Bool</span></a></span>, which denotes a boolean.<a href=\"#p_57\" class=\"pid\">57</a></li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_58\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_UInt\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"UInt\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span>, which denotes an unsigned integer.\n    <span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_UInt.max\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"UInt.max\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">UInt</span></a><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt.max\" title=\"rsh: UInt.max\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.max</span></a></span> is the largest value that may be assigned to a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_58\" class=\"pid\">58</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_59\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_UInt256\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"UInt256\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt256\" title=\"rsh: UInt256\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt256</span></a></span>, which denotes an unsigned integer with 256 bits.\n    <span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_UInt256.max\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"UInt256.max\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt256\" title=\"rsh: UInt256\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">UInt256</span></a><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt256.max\" title=\"rsh: UInt256.max\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.max</span></a></span> is the largest value that may be assigned to a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt256\" title=\"rsh: UInt256\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt256</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_59\" class=\"pid\">59</a>\n  </li>\n  <li><i id=\"p_60\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Int\" title=\"rsh: Int\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Int</span></a></span>, which denotes a signed integer.<a href=\"#p_60\" class=\"pid\">60</a></li>\n  <li><i id=\"p_61\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_FixedPoint\" title=\"rsh: FixedPoint\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">FixedPoint</span></a></span>, which denotes a fractional number.<a href=\"#p_61\" class=\"pid\">61</a></li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_62\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Bytes\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Bytes\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Bytes\" title=\"rsh: Bytes\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Bytes</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(length)</span></span>, which denotes a sequence of bytes of length at most <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_length\" title=\"rsh: length\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">length</span></a></span>.\n    Bytes of different lengths are not compatible; however the shorter bytes may be <a href=\"/rsh/compute/#padding\">padded</a>.<a href=\"#p_62\" class=\"pid\">62</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_63\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_BytesDyn\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"BytesDyn\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_BytesDyn\" title=\"rsh: BytesDyn\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">BytesDyn</span></a></span>, which denotes a sequence of bytes of dynamic length.\n    Bytes of fixed length and bytes of dynamic length are totally incompatible, but bytes of fixed length can be casted into <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_BytesDyn\" title=\"rsh: BytesDyn\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">BytesDyn</span></a></span> with <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_BytesDyn\" title=\"rsh: BytesDyn\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">BytesDyn</span></a></span> applied as a function.<a href=\"#p_63\" class=\"pid\">63</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_64\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_StringDyn\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"StringDyn\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_StringDyn\" title=\"rsh: StringDyn\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">StringDyn</span></a></span>, which denotes a string of UTF-8 code points of dynamic length.\n    Strings and bytes are totally incompatible, but static bytes can be casted into dynamic strings with <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_StringDyn\" title=\"rsh: StringDyn\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">StringDyn</span></a></span> applied as function.<a href=\"#p_64\" class=\"pid\">64</a>\n  </li>\n  <li><i id=\"p_65\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Digest\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Digest\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Digest\" title=\"rsh: Digest\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Digest</span></a></span>, which denotes a digest.<a href=\"#p_65\" class=\"pid\">65</a></li>\n  <li><i id=\"p_66\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Address\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Address\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Address\" title=\"rsh: Address\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Address</span></a></span>, which denotes an account address.<a href=\"#p_66\" class=\"pid\">66</a></li>\n  <li><i id=\"p_67\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Contract\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Contract\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Contract\" title=\"rsh: Contract\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Contract</span></a></span>, which denotes the identifying information of a contract.<a href=\"#p_67\" class=\"pid\">67</a></li>\n</ul>\n<div class=\"note\">\n  <p>\n    <i id=\"p_68\" class=\"pid\"></i>Reach has different representations of contracts across connectors.\n    For example, on Algorand a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Contract\" title=\"rsh: Contract\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Contract</span></a></span> is an Application ID, but on Ethereum it is an Address.<a href=\"#p_68\" class=\"pid\">68</a>\n  </p>\n</div>\n<ul>\n  <li><i id=\"p_69\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Token\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Token\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Token\" title=\"rsh: Token\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Token</span></a></span>, which denotes a non-network token. <a href=\"/networks/#ref-networks\">Networks</a> discusses how <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Token\" title=\"rsh: Token\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Token</span></a></span>s are represented on specific networks.<a href=\"#p_69\" class=\"pid\">69</a></li>\n</ul>\n<div class=\"note\">\n  <p>\n    <i id=\"p_70\" class=\"pid\"></i>Reach assumes that every <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Token\" title=\"rsh: Token\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Token</span></a></span> in your program refers to a different non-network token.\n    It will automatically insert <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_require\" title=\"rsh: require\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">require</span></a></span> statements that enforce this constraint.<a href=\"#p_70\" class=\"pid\">70</a>\n  </p>\n</div>\n<ul>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_71\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Fun\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Fun\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Fun\" title=\"rsh: Fun\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Fun</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">([Domain_0</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">...</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Domain_N]</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Range)</span></span>, which denotes a <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_function%20type\">function type</span>, when <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Domain_i</span></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Range</span></span> are types.\n    The domain of a function is negative position.\n    The range of a function is positive position.<a href=\"#p_71\" class=\"pid\">71</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_72\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Fun\" title=\"rsh: Fun\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Fun</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Range)</span></span>, which denotes an <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_unconstrained%20domain%20function%20type\">unconstrained domain function type</span>, when <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Range</span></span> is a type.\n    These functions may only appear in participant interact interfaces.<a href=\"#p_72\" class=\"pid\">72</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_73\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Tuple\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Tuple\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Tuple\" title=\"rsh: Tuple\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Tuple</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(Field_0</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">...</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> FieldN)</span></span>, which denotes a tuple.\n    (Refer to <a href=\"/rsh/compute/#ref-programs-tuples\">Tuples</a> for constructing tuples.)<a href=\"#p_73\" class=\"pid\">73</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_74\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Object\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Object\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Object\" title=\"rsh: Object\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Object</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">({key_0</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Type_0</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">...</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> key_N</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Type_N})</span></span>, which denotes an object.\n    (Refer to <a href=\"/rsh/compute/#ref-programs-objects\">Objects</a> for constructing objects.)<a href=\"#p_74\" class=\"pid\">74</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_75\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Struct\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Struct\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Struct\" title=\"rsh: Struct\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Struct</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">([[key_0</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Type_0]</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">...</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> [key_N</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Type_N]])</span></span>, which denotes a struct.\n    (Refer to <a href=\"/rsh/compute/#ref-programs-structs\">Structs</a> for constructing structs.)<a href=\"#p_75\" class=\"pid\">75</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_76\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Array\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Array\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Array\" title=\"rsh: Array\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Array</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(Type_0</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> size)</span></span>, which denotes a statically-sized array.\n    <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Type_0</span></span> must be a type that can exist at runtime (i.e., not a function type.)\n    (Refer to <a href=\"/rsh/compute/#ref-programs-arrays\">Arrays</a> for constructing arrays.)<a href=\"#p_76\" class=\"pid\">76</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_77\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Data\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Data\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Data\" title=\"rsh: Data\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Data</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">({variant_0</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Type_0</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">...</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> variant_N</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Type_N})</span></span>, which denotes a <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tagged_union\">tagged union</a> (or <em>sum type</em>).\n    (Refer to <a href=\"/rsh/compute/#ref-programs-data\">Data</a> for constructing data instances.)<a href=\"#p_77\" class=\"pid\">77</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_78\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Refine\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Refine\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Refine\" title=\"rsh: Refine\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Refine</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(Type_0</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Predicate</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_?\" title=\"rsh: ?\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">?</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Message)</span></span>, where <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Predicate</span></span> is a unary function returning a boolean, which denotes a <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Refinement_type\">refinement type</a>, that is instances of <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Type_0</span></span> that satisfy <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Predicate</span></span>.\n    When a refinement type appears in a <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_negative%20position\">negative position</span> (such as in an <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_is\" title=\"rsh: is\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">is</span></a></span> or in the domain of a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Fun\" title=\"rsh: Fun\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Fun</span></a></span> of a participant interact interface), it introduces an <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_assert\" title=\"rsh: assert\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">assert</span></a></span>;\n    while when it is in a <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_positive%20position\">positive position</span>, it introduces an <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/local/#rsh_assume\" title=\"rsh: assume\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">assume</span></a></span>.\n    <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Message</span></span> is an optional string to display if the predicate fails verification.<a href=\"#p_78\" class=\"pid\">78</a>\n  </li>\n</ul>\n<p><i id=\"p_79\" class=\"pid\"></i>For example, if <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">f</span></span> had type<a href=\"#p_79\" class=\"pid\">79</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"Fun([Refine(UInt, (x => x < 5))], Refine(UInt, (x => x > 10)))\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn26\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Fun\" title=\"rsh: Fun\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Fun</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">([</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Refine\" title=\"rsh: Refine\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Refine</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(UInt</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> (x </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_=%3E\" title=\"rsh: =>\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=&gt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> x </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%3C\" title=\"rsh: <\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&lt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">5</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">))]</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Refine\" title=\"rsh: Refine\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Refine</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(UInt</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> (x </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_=%3E\" title=\"rsh: =>\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=&gt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> x </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%3E\" title=\"rsh: >\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&gt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">10</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">)))</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p><i id=\"p_80\" class=\"pid\"></i>then <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">z</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">f</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(y)</span></span> is equivalent to<a href=\"#p_80\" class=\"pid\">80</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"assert(y < 5);\nconst z = f(y);\nassume(z > 10);\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn27\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_assert\" title=\"rsh: assert\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">assert</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(y </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%3C\" title=\"rsh: <\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&lt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">5</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">);</span></li><li value=\"2\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">z</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">f</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(y);</span></li><li value=\"3\"><a href=\"/rsh/local/#rsh_assume\" title=\"rsh: assume\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">assume</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(z </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%3E\" title=\"rsh: >\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&gt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">10</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<ul>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_81\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Refine\" title=\"rsh: Refine\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Refine</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(Type_0</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> PreCondition</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> PostCondition</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_?\" title=\"rsh: ?\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">?</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Messages)</span></span>, where <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Type_0</span></span> is a function type, <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">PreCondition</span></span> is a unary function that accepts a tuple of the domain and returns a boolean, and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">PostCondition</span></span> is a binary function that accepts a tuple of the domain and the range and returns a boolean, denotes a function type with a <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Precondition\">precondition</a> and <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Postcondition\">postcondition</a>.\n    Preconditions are enforced with <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_assert\" title=\"rsh: assert\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">assert</span></a></span> and postconditions are enforced with <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/local/#rsh_assume\" title=\"rsh: assume\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">assume</span></a></span>.\n    <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Messages</span></span> is an optional two-tuple of <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Bytes\" title=\"rsh: Bytes\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Bytes</span></a></span>.\n    The first message will be displayed when the precondition fails verification and the second when the postcondition fails verification.<a href=\"#p_81\" class=\"pid\">81</a>\n  </li>\n</ul>\n<p><i id=\"p_82\" class=\"pid\"></i>For example, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Refine\" title=\"rsh: Refine\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Refine</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Fun\" title=\"rsh: Fun\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Fun</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">([UInt</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> UInt]</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> UInt)</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> ([x</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> y] </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_=%3E\" title=\"rsh: =>\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=&gt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> x </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%3C\" title=\"rsh: <\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&lt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> y)</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> (([x</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> y]</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> z) </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_=%3E\" title=\"rsh: =>\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=&gt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> x </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_+\" title=\"rsh: +\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">+</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> y </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%3C\" title=\"rsh: <\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&lt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> z))</span></span> is a function that requires its second argument to be larger than its first and its result to be larger than its input.<a href=\"#p_82\" class=\"pid\">82</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_83\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Object\" title=\"rsh: Object\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Object</span></a></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Data\" title=\"rsh: Data\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Data</span></a></span> are commonly used to implemented <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algebraic_data_type\">algebraic data types</a> in Reach.<a href=\"#p_83\" class=\"pid\">83</a></p>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_typeOf\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"typeOf\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_isType\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"isType\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_is\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"is\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"typeOf(x) // type\nisType(t) // Bool\nis(x, t) // t\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn28\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_typeOf\" title=\"rsh: typeOf\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">typeOf</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(x) </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// type</span></li><li value=\"2\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_isType\" title=\"rsh: isType\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">isType</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(t) </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// Bool</span></li><li value=\"3\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_is\" title=\"rsh: is\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">is</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(x</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> t) </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// t</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_84\" class=\"pid\"></i>The <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_typeOf\" title=\"rsh: typeOf\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">typeOf</span></a></span> primitive function is the same as <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_typeof\" title=\"rsh: typeof\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">typeof</span></a></span>:\n  it returns the type of its argument.<a href=\"#p_84\" class=\"pid\">84</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_85\" class=\"pid\"></i>The <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_isType\" title=\"rsh: isType\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">isType</span></a></span> function returns <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></span> if its argument is a type.\n  Any expression satisfying <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_isType\" title=\"rsh: isType\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">isType</span></a></span> is compiled away and does not exist at runtime.<a href=\"#p_85\" class=\"pid\">85</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_86\" class=\"pid\"></i>The <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_is\" title=\"rsh: is\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">is</span></a></span> function returns its first argument if it satisfies the type specified by the second argument.\n  If it is not, then the program is invalid.\n  For example, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_is\" title=\"rsh: is\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">is</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">5</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> UInt)</span></span> returns <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">5</span></span>, while <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_is\" title=\"rsh: is\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">is</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">5</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Bool)</span></span> is an invalid program.\n  The value returned by <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_is\" title=\"rsh: is\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">is</span></a></span> may not be identical to the input, because in some cases, such as for functions, it will record the applied to type and enforce it on future invocations.\n  These applications are considered negative positions for <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Refine\" title=\"rsh: Refine\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Refine</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_86\" class=\"pid\">86</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"literal-values\" class=\"refHeader\">Literal values<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#literal-values\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_true\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"true\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_false\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"false\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_null\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"null\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"10\n0xdeadbeef\n007\n-10\n34.5432\n123_456_789\n0x12_34_56\ntrue\nfalse\nnull\n&quot;reality bytes&quot;\n'it just does'\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn29\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">10</span></li><li value=\"2\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">0xdeadbeef</span></li><li value=\"3\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">007</span></li><li value=\"4\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_-\" title=\"rsh: -\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">-</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">10</span></li><li value=\"5\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">34.5432</span></li><li value=\"6\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">123_456_789</span></li><li value=\"7\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">0x12_34_56</span></li><li value=\"8\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></li><li value=\"9\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_false\" title=\"rsh: false\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">false</span></a></li><li value=\"10\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_null\" title=\"rsh: null\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">null</span></a></li><li value=\"11\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">\"reality bytes\"</span></li><li value=\"12\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'it just does'</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_87\" class=\"pid\"></i>A <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_literal%20value\">literal value</span>,\n  written <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">VALUE</span></span>,\n  is an expression that evaluates to the given value.<a href=\"#p_87\" class=\"pid\">87</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_88\" class=\"pid\"></i>The <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_null%20literal\">null literal</span> may be written as <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_null\" title=\"rsh: null\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">null</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_88\" class=\"pid\">88</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_89\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"term\" id=\"term_Numeric%20literal\">Numeric literal</span>s may be written in decimal, hexadecimal, octal, or scientific (exponential) notation.\n  Numeric literals must obey the <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_bit%20width\">bit width</span> of <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span> if they are used as <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span> values at runtime, but if they only appear at compile-time, then they may be any positive number.\n  Reach provides abstractions for working with <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Int\" title=\"rsh: Int\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Int</span></a></span>s and signed <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_FixedPoint\" title=\"rsh: FixedPoint\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">FixedPoint</span></a></span> numbers.\n  <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Int\" title=\"rsh: Int\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Int</span></a></span>s may be defined by applying the unary <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_+\" title=\"rsh: +\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">+</span></a></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_-\" title=\"rsh: -\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">-</span></a></span> operators to values of type <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span>.\n  Reach provides syntactic sugar for defining signed <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_FixedPoint\" title=\"rsh: FixedPoint\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">FixedPoint</span></a></span> numbers, in base 10, with decimal syntax.\n  Numeric literals may contain underscore separators as a visual aid (e.g. <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">123_456</span></span> is the same as <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">123456</span></span>).<a href=\"#p_89\" class=\"pid\">89</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_90\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"term\" id=\"term_Exponential%20notation\">Exponential notation</span> may be written as <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%3C\" title=\"rsh: <\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">&lt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">coefficient</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">&gt;(e|E)&lt;</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">exponent</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%3E\" title=\"rsh: >\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">&gt;</span></a></span>, where <code>coefficient</code> may be of type <code>UInt, Int, or FixedPoint</code> and <code>exponent</code> may be of type <code>UInt | Int</code>.\n  The evaluated number will have the precision of the coefficient or negative exponent, whichever is more precise.\n  Below are examples of exponential notation:<a href=\"#p_90\" class=\"pid\">90</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a href=\"https://github.com/reach-sh/reach-lang/tree/master/hs/t/y/exponential-notation.rsh\">/hs/t/y/exponential-notation.rsh</a><a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"  // pos coefficient, pos exponent, lower `e`\n  assert(1e4 === 10_000);\n  // neg coefficient, pos exponent, upper `e`\n  assert(-5E8 === -500_000_000);\n  // neg coefficient, neg exponent\n  assert(-23E-4 === -0.0023);\n  // coefficient specifies 0 decimal precision\n  assert(1.e2 === 100);\n  // coefficient specifies 1 decimal precision\n  assert(1.1e2 === 110.0);\n  // coefficient specifies 2 decimal precision\n  assert(1.22e1 === 12.20);\n  // neg exponent specifies 3 decimal precision\n  assert(3e-3 === 0.003);\n  // coefficient precision > exponent precision\n  assert(12.3456e-2 === .1234);\n  // coefficient precision < exponent precision\n  assert(12.34e-3 === .012);\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn30\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">.012</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p><i id=\"p_91\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"term\" id=\"term_Boolean%20literal\">Boolean literal</span>s may be written as <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></span> or <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_false\" title=\"rsh: false\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">false</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_91\" class=\"pid\">91</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_92\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"term\" id=\"term_String%20literal\">String literal</span>s (aka byte strings)\n  may be written between double or single quotes\n  (with no distinction between the different styles)\n  and use the same escaping rules as JavaScript.\n  Since <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Bytes\" title=\"rsh: Bytes\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Bytes</span></a></span> types are specialized in their length, literals typically need to be <a href=\"/rsh/compute/#padding\">padded</a> to be useful.<a href=\"#p_92\" class=\"pid\">92</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_93\" class=\"pid\"></i>Static byte strings can be converted into static strings by calling <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_StringDyn\" title=\"rsh: StringDyn\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">StringDyn</span></a></span> as a function, like <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_StringDyn\" title=\"rsh: StringDyn\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">StringDyn</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">\"normally bytes\"</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">)</span></span>.<a href=\"#p_93\" class=\"pid\">93</a></p>\n<h3 id=\"operator-expression\" class=\"refHeader\">Operator expression<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#operator-expression\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_94\" class=\"pid\"></i>An <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_operator\">operator</span> is a special identifier,\n  which is either a unary operator, or a binary operator.<a href=\"#p_94\" class=\"pid\">94</a>\n</p>\n<hr>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_!\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"!\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_-\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"-\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_+\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"+\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_typeof\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"typeof\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_not\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"not\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_minus\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"minus\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_plus\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"plus\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_void\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"void\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"! a  // not\n- a  // minus\n+ a  // plus\ntypeof a\nvoid a\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn31\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_!\" title=\"rsh: !\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">!</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> a  </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// not</span></li><li value=\"2\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_-\" title=\"rsh: -\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">-</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> a  </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// minus</span></li><li value=\"3\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_+\" title=\"rsh: +\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">+</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> a  </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// plus</span></li><li value=\"4\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_typeof\" title=\"rsh: typeof\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">typeof</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> a</span></li><li value=\"5\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_void\" title=\"rsh: void\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">void</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> a</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_95\" class=\"pid\"></i>A <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_unary%20expression\">unary expression</span>, written <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">UNAOP</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> EXPR_rhs</span></span>, where <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">EXPR_rhs</span></span> is an expression and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">UNAOP</span></span> is one of the <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_unary%20operator\">unary operator</span>s: <code>! - + typeof void</code>. All the unary operators, besides <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_typeof\" title=\"rsh: typeof\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">typeof</span></a></span>, have a\n  corresponding named version in the standard library.<a href=\"#p_95\" class=\"pid\">95</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_96\" class=\"pid\"></i>It is invalid to use unary operations on the wrong types of values.<a href=\"#p_96\" class=\"pid\">96</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_97\" class=\"pid\"></i>When applied to values of type <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span>, unary <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_-\" title=\"rsh: -\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">-</span></a></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_+\" title=\"rsh: +\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">+</span></a></span> operators will cast\n  their arguments to type <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Int\" title=\"rsh: Int\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Int</span></a></span>. The unary <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_-\" title=\"rsh: -\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">-</span></a></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_+\" title=\"rsh: +\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">+</span></a></span> operations are defined for\n  values of type: <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Int\" title=\"rsh: Int\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Int</span></a></span>, and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_FixedPoint\" title=\"rsh: FixedPoint\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">FixedPoint</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_97\" class=\"pid\">97</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_98\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_void\" title=\"rsh: void\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">void</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> a</span></span> evaluates to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_null\" title=\"rsh: null\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">null</span></a></span> for all arguments.<a href=\"#p_98\" class=\"pid\">98</a></p>\n<hr>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_&amp;&amp;\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"&amp;&amp;\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_%7C%7C\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"||\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_+\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"+\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_-\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"-\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_*\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"*\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_/\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"/\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_%25\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"%\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_%7C\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"|\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_&amp;\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"&amp;\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_%5E\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"^\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_%3C%3C\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"<<\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_%3E%3E\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\">>\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_==\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"==\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_!=\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"!=\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_===\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"===\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_!==\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"!==\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_%3E\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\">\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_%3E=\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\">=\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_%3C=\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"<=\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_%3C\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"<\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"a &amp;&amp; b\na || b\na + b\na - b\na * b\na / b\na % b\na | b\na &amp; b\na ^ b\na << b\na >> b\na == b\na != b\na === b\na !== b\na > b\na >= b\na <= b\na < b\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn32\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a </span><a style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"3\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_+\" title=\"rsh: +\"><span style=\"color: href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_-\" title=\"rsh: -\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">-</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"5\"><span var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"6\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_/\" title=\"rsh: /\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">/</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"7\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%25\" title=\"rsh: %\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">%</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"8\"><span var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"9\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_&amp;\" title=\"rsh: &amp;\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&amp;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"10\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%5E\" title=\"rsh: ^\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">^</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"11\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%3C%3C\" title=\"rsh: <<\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&lt;&lt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"12\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%3E%3E\" title=\"rsh: >>\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&gt;&gt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"13\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_==\" title=\"rsh: ==\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">==</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"14\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_!=\" title=\"rsh: !=\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">!=</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"15\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_===\" title=\"rsh: ===\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">===</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"16\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_!==\" title=\"rsh: !==\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">!==</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"17\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%3E\" title=\"rsh: >\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&gt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"18\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%3E=\" title=\"rsh: >=\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&gt;=</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"19\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%3C=\" title=\"rsh: <=\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&lt;=</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li><li value=\"20\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%3C\" title=\"rsh: <\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&lt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span></li></ol></pre>\n<div class=\"note\">\n  <p><i id=\"p_99\" class=\"pid\"></i>Bitwise operations are not supported by all consensus networks and greatly decrease the efficiency of verification.<a href=\"#p_99\" class=\"pid\">99</a></p>\n</div>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_100\" class=\"pid\"></i>A <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_binary%20expression\">binary expression</span> is written <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">EXPR_lhs </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">BINOP</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> EXPR_rhs</span></span>, where <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">EXPR_lhs</span></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">EXPR_rhs</span></span> are expressions and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">BINOP</span></span> is one of the <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_binary%20operator\">binary operator</span>s: <code>&amp;&amp; || + - * / % | &amp; ^ &lt;&lt; &gt;&gt; == != === !== &gt; &gt;= &lt;= &lt;</code>.\n  Numeric operations, like <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_+\" title=\"rsh: +\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">+</span></a></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%3E\" title=\"rsh: >\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&gt;</span></a></span>, only operate on numbers.\n  Since all numbers in Reach are integers, operations like <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_/\" title=\"rsh: /\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">/</span></a></span> truncate their result.\n  Boolean operations, like <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_&amp;&amp;\" title=\"rsh: &amp;&amp;\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&amp;&amp;</span></a></span>, only operate on booleans.\n  <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_xor\" title=\"rsh: xor\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">xor</span></a></span> operates on <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span>s, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt256\" title=\"rsh: UInt256\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt256</span></a></span>s, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Bool\" title=\"rsh: Bool\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Bool</span></a></span>s, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Digest\" title=\"rsh: Digest\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Digest</span></a></span>s, and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Bytes\" title=\"rsh: Bytes\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Bytes</span></a></span> of the same length.\n  <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_polyMod\" title=\"rsh: polyMod\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">polyMod</span></a></span> operates on <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span>s and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt256\" title=\"rsh: UInt256\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt256</span></a></span>. The first argument may be a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Digest\" title=\"rsh: Digest\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Digest</span></a></span> or <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Bytes\" title=\"rsh: Bytes\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Bytes</span></a></span>.\n  It is invalid to use binary operations on the wrong types of values.<a href=\"#p_100\" class=\"pid\">100</a>\n</p>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_and\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"and\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_or\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"or\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_xor\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"xor\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_add\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"add\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_sub\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"sub\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_mul\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"mul\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_div\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"div\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_mod\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"mod\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_polyMod\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"polyMod\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_eq\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"eq\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_lt\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"lt\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_le\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"le\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_ge\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"ge\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_gt\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"gt\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_lsh\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"lsh\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_rsh\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"rsh\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_band\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"band\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_bior\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"bior\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_bxor\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"bxor\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_polyEq\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"polyEq\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_polyNeq\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"polyNeq\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_safeAdd\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"safeAdd\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_safeSub\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"safeSub\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_safeMul\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"safeMul\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_safeDiv\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"safeDiv\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_safeMod\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"safeMod\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_veriAdd\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"veriAdd\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_veriSub\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"veriSub\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_veriMul\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"veriMul\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_veriDiv\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"veriDiv\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_veriMod\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"veriMod\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"and(a, b)     // &amp;&amp;\nor(a, b)      // ||\nxor(a, b)     // ^\nadd(a, b)     // +\nsub(a, b)     // -\nmul(a, b)     // *\ndiv(a, b)     // /\npolyMod(a, b) // %\neq(a, b)      // ==\nlt(a, b)      // <\nle(a, b)      // <=\nge(a, b)      // >=\ngt(a, b)      // >\nlsh(a, b)     // <<\nrsh(a, b)     // >>\nband(a, b)    // &amp;\nbior(a, b)    // |\npolyEq(a, b)  // ==, ===\npolyNeq(a, b) // !=, !==\nsafeAdd(a, b)\nsafeSub(a, b)\nsafeMul(a, b)\nsafeDiv(a, b)\nsafeMod(a, b)\nveriAdd(a, b)\nveriSub(a, b)\nveriMul(a, b)\nveriDiv(a, b)\nveriMod(a, b)\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn33\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_and\" title=\"rsh: and\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">and</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(a</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b)     </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// &amp;&amp;</span></li><li value=\"2\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_or\" title=\"rsh: or\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">or</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b)</span></li><li value=\"29\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_veriMod\" title=\"rsh: veriMod\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">veriMod</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(a</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b)</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_101\" class=\"pid\"></i>All binary expression operators have a corresponding named function in the standard library.\n  The named arithmetic functions prefixed with <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">safe</span></span>, e.g. <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_safeAdd\" title=\"rsh: safeAdd\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">safeAdd</span></a></span>, bypass <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_verifyArithmetic\" title=\"rsh: verifyArithmetic\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">verifyArithmetic</span></a></span> and are not statically verified; they are only checked at runtime.\n  The named arithmetic functions prefixed with <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">veri</span></span>, e.g. <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_veriAdd\" title=\"rsh: veriAdd\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">veriAdd</span></a></span>, are statically verified, regardless of <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_verifyArithmetic\" title=\"rsh: verifyArithmetic\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">verifyArithmetic</span></a></span>; no runtime checks will be generated for these verified operations.\n  The <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">veri</span></span> functions enable you to verify arithmetic in specific parts of a program, as opposed to using <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_verifyArithmetic\" title=\"rsh: verifyArithmetic\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">verifyArithmetic</span></a></span> throughout the whole application.\n  While <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_&amp;&amp;\" title=\"rsh: &amp;&amp;\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&amp;&amp;</span></a></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_%7C%7C\" title=\"rsh: ||\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">||</span></a></span> may not evaluate their second argument,\n  their corresponding named functions <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_and\" title=\"rsh: and\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">and</span></a></span>, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_or\" title=\"rsh: or\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">or</span></a></span>, and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_xor\" title=\"rsh: xor\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">xor</span></a></span>, always do.<a href=\"#p_101\" class=\"pid\">101</a>\n</p>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_boolEq\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"boolEq\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_typeEq\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"typeEq\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_intEq\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"intEq\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_digestEq\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"digestEq\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_addressEq\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"addressEq\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_fxeq\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"fxeq\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_ieq\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"ieq\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far
