var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// eq on Int</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_102\" class=\"pid\"></i>Equality functions, like <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_==\" title=\"rsh: ==\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">==</span></a></span>, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_===\" title=\"rsh: ===\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">===</span></a></span>, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_!=\" title=\"rsh: !=\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">!=</span></a></span>, and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_!==\" title=\"rsh: !==\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">!==</span></a></span>, operate on all types.\n  However, values with different types are always not equal.\n  Both arguments must be of the same type.\n  Specialized functions exist for equality checking on each supported type.<a href=\"#p_102\" class=\"pid\">102</a>\n</p>\n<hr>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_103\" class=\"pid\"></i>If <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_verifyArithmetic\" title=\"rsh: verifyArithmetic\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">verifyArithmetic</span></a></span> is <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></span>, then arithmetic operations automatically make a static assertion that their arguments would not overflow the bit width of the enabled consensus networks.\n  If it is <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_false\" title=\"rsh: false\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">false</span></a></span>, then the connector will ensure this dynamically.<a href=\"#p_103\" class=\"pid\">103</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"numeric-casting\" class=\"refHeader\">Numeric Casting<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#numeric-casting\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_104\" class=\"pid\"></i>Reach has different unsigned integer types, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt256\" title=\"rsh: UInt256\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt256</span></a></span>.\n  These values can be casted from one to the other by calling the type as a function with a value.<a href=\"#p_104\" class=\"pid\">104</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_105\" class=\"pid\"></i>For example, if <code>x</code> is a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span>, then <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt256\" title=\"rsh: UInt256\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">UInt256</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(x)</span></span> is <code>x</code> zero-extended to 256 bits.\n  This is demonstrated in the code below:<a href=\"#p_105\" class=\"pid\">105</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a href=\"https://github.com/reach-sh/reach-lang/tree/master/examples/uint256/index.rsh\">/examples/uint256/index.rsh</a><a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"    vs1: Tuple(UInt256, UInt256, UInt, UInt),\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn35\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"79\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">    vs1</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Tuple\" title=\"rsh: Tuple\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Tuple</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(UInt256</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> UInt256</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> UInt</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> UInt)</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span></li></ol></pre>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a href=\"https://github.com/reach-sh/reach-lang/tree/master/examples/uint256/index.rsh\">/examples/uint256/index.rsh</a><a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"  const [b1, b2, s1, s2] = vs1;\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn36\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"88\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">  </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> [</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">b1</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">b2</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">s1</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">s2</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">] </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> vs1;</span></li></ol></pre>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a href=\"https://github.com/reach-sh/reach-lang/tree/master/examples/uint256/index.rsh\">/examples/uint256/index.rsh</a><a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"  const s1b = UInt256(s1);\n  const s2b = UInt256(s2);\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn37\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"92\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">  </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt256\" title=\"rsh: UInt256\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">UInt256</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(s1);</span></li><li value=\"93\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">  </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">s2b</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt256\" title=\"rsh: UInt256\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">UInt256</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(s2);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_106\" class=\"pid\"></i>However, if <code>y</code> is a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt256\" title=\"rsh: UInt256\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt256</span></a></span>, then <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">UInt</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(y)</span></span> is <code>y</code> with as many bits as <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span> has.\n  This is demonstrated in the code below:<a href=\"#p_106\" class=\"pid\">106</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a href=\"https://github.com/reach-sh/reach-lang/tree/master/hs/t/y/uint256-verify2.rsh\">/hs/t/y/uint256-verify2.rsh</a><a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"    x: UInt256,\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn38\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"6\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">    x</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> UInt256</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span></li></ol></pre>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a href=\"https://github.com/reach-sh/reach-lang/tree/master/hs/t/y/uint256-verify2.rsh\">/hs/t/y/uint256-verify2.rsh</a><a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"    const y = UInt(x);\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn39\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"12\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">    </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">y</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">UInt</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(x);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_107\" class=\"pid\"></i>In the second case above, where <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt256\" title=\"rsh: UInt256\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt256</span></a></span> is casted to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span>, if <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt256\" title=\"rsh: UInt256\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt256</span></a></span> has any non-zero bits that would be lost by the truncation, then the cast will fail at runtime.\n  This is guaranteed to not happen when you compile with <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_verifyArithmetic\" title=\"rsh: verifyArithmetic\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">verifyArithmetic</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_107\" class=\"pid\">107</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_108\" class=\"pid\"></i>If you wish to explicitly truncate a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span>* type into a smaller size, you can pass a second, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Bool\" title=\"rsh: Bool\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Bool</span></a></span> argument to the cast call.\n  Passing <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></span> truncates the number.\n  Passing <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_false\" title=\"rsh: false\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">false</span></a></span> causes the cast to fail, as describe above.\n  This is the default behavior.<a href=\"#p_108\" class=\"pid\">108</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"const x = UInt256(/* big number */);\nconst x_truncated = UInt(x, true);\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn40\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">x</span><span style=\"color: */</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">);</span></li><li value=\"2\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">UInt</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(x</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_109\" class=\"pid\"></i>You may specify a third argument, that is of type <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Bool\" title=\"rsh: Bool\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Bool</span></a></span>, when performing a cast.\n  When <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></span>, the cast will be statically verified.\n  When <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_false\" title=\"rsh: false\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">false</span></a></span>, the cast will only be checked at runtime.\n  If unspecified, it will default to whatever <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_verifyArithmetic\" title=\"rsh: verifyArithmetic\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">verifyArithmetic</span></a></span> is set to.<a href=\"#p_109\" class=\"pid\">109</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_110\" class=\"pid\"></i>Numeric literals in your program are considered <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span>.\n  If they are cast to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt256\" title=\"rsh: UInt256\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt256</span></a></span>, then your program can contain constant <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt256\" title=\"rsh: UInt256\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt256</span></a></span> values.<a href=\"#p_110\" class=\"pid\">110</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"string-conversion\" class=\"refHeader\">String Conversion<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#string-conversion\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_111\" class=\"pid\"></i>Some values, specifically unsigned integers and bytes, can be converted into dynamically sized strings by calling <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_StringDyn\" title=\"rsh: StringDyn\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">StringDyn</span></a></span> as a function.\n  For example:<a href=\"#p_111\" class=\"pid\">111</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"&quot;Four&quot; // => the bytes &quot;Four&quot; (i.e. 46, 6F, 75, 72)\nStringDyn(&quot;Four&quot;) // => the string &quot;Four&quot; (same var(--shiki-color-text)\">) </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// =&gt; \"4\"</span></li></ol></pre>\n<h3 id=\"contract-and-address-comparisons\" class=\"refHeader\">Contract and var(--shiki-token-function)\">getAddress</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">())</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_112\" class=\"pid\"></i>Although <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Contract\" title=\"rsh: Contract\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Contract</span></a></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Address\" title=\"rsh: Address\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Address</span></a></span> are not necessarily the same\n  type, they often have a connection.\n  <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Contract\" title=\"rsh: Contract\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Contract</span></a><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Contract.addressEq\" title=\"rsh: Contract.addressEq\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.addressEq</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(ctc</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> addr)</span></span> returns a boolean that is <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></span>\n  if <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">ctc</span></span> refers to the same contract as <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">addr</span></span>.<a href=\"#p_112\" class=\"pid\">112</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"boolxor\" class=\"refHeader\">boolXor<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#boolxor\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_boolXor\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"boolXor\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"boolXor(false, false); // false\nboolXor(false, true);  // true\nboolXor(true, false);  // true\nboolXor(true, true);   // false\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn43\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_boolXor\" title=\"rsh: boolXor\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">boolXor</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_false\" title=\"rsh: false\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">false</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_false\" title=\"rsh: false\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">false</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">); </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// false</span></li><li value=\"2\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_boolXor\" title=\"rsh: boolXor\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">boolXor</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_false\" title=\"rsh: false\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">false</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">);  </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// true</span></li><li value=\"3\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_boolXor\" title=\"rsh: boolXor\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">boolXor</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_false\" title=\"rsh: false\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">false</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">);  </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// true</span></li><li value=\"4\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_boolXor\" title=\"rsh: boolXor\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">boolXor</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">);   </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// false</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_113\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_boolXor\" title=\"rsh: boolXor\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">boolXor</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(Bool</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Bool)</span></span> returns <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></span> only when the inputs differ in value.\n  This function is specialized to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Bool\" title=\"rsh: Bool\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Bool</span></a></span>s; <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_xor\" title=\"rsh: xor\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">xor</span></a></span> supports more types.<a href=\"#p_113\" class=\"pid\">113</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"padding\" class=\"refHeader\">Padding<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#padding\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Bytes.pad\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Bytes.pad\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"Bytes(16).pad('abc');\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn44\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Bytes\" title=\"rsh: Bytes\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Bytes</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">16</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">)</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Bytes.pad\" title=\"rsh: Bytes.pad\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.pad</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'abc'</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_114\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Bytes\" title=\"rsh: Bytes\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Bytes</span></a></span> are like <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Array\" title=\"rsh: Array\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Array</span></a></span>s in that they are fixed and exactly sized.\n  This means that two <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Bytes\" title=\"rsh: Bytes\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Bytes</span></a></span> of different lengths are not interchangeable.<a href=\"#p_114\" class=\"pid\">114</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_115\" class=\"pid\"></i>For example, <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'You win!'</span></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'You lose!'</span></span> cannot both be provided to an <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/local/#rsh_interact\" title=\"rsh: interact\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">interact</span></a></span> function, because the second is one character longer.\n  Most of the time this is good, because it is a signal that you should use a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Data\" title=\"rsh: Data\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Data</span></a></span> type instead, so that the formatting and display logic is entirely controlled by the frontend.<a href=\"#p_115\" class=\"pid\">115</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_116\" class=\"pid\"></i>But, sometimes it is necessary and useful to extend one byte string into a larger size.\n  Each <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Bytes\" title=\"rsh: Bytes\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Bytes</span></a></span> type has a <code>pad</code> field that is bound to a function that extends its argument to the needed size.\n  A byte string extended in this way is called <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_padded\">padded</span>, because it is extended with additional <code>NUL</code> bytes at the end of the string.<a href=\"#p_116\" class=\"pid\">116</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_117\" class=\"pid\"></i>The code below shows how <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Padding</span></span> can be done:<a href=\"#p_117\" class=\"pid\">117</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a ]\n[ 1, 2 + 3, 4 * 5 ]\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn50\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">[ ]</span></li><li style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">n</span></span> values, where <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">EXPR_0</span></span> through <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">...</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">expr</span></span> may appear inside tuple expressions, in which case the spreaded expression must evaluate to a tuple or array, which is spliced in place.<a href=\"#p_122\" class=\"pid\">122</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a (<code>loanAmt</code>, <code>interest</code>, <code>nft</code>, and <code>deadline</code>) that are created at the same time, and then a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/local/#rsh_declassify\" title=\"rsh: declassify\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">declassify</span></a></span> is performed to make them knowable to other users.<a href=\"#p_123\" class=\"pid\">123</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"ref-programs-arrays\" class=\"refHeader\">Arrays<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#ref-programs-arrays\"><span class=\"icon id=\"term_array\">array</span>.<a href=\"#p_124\" class=\"pid\">124</a></p>\n<h3 id=\"element-reference\" class=\"refHeader\">Element reference<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#element-reference\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"arr[3]\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn53\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">arr[</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">3</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">]</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_125\" class=\"pid\"></i>A <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_reference\">reference</span>, written <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">REF_EXPR</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">[</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">IDX_EXPR</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">]</span></span>,\n  where <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">REF_EXPR</span></span> is an expression that evaluates to an array, a tuple, an object, or a struct\n  and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">IDX_EXPR</span></span> is an expression that evaluates to a natural number which is less than the size of the array,\n  selects the element at the given index of the array.\n  Indices start at zero.<a href=\"#p_125\" class=\"pid\">125</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_126\" class=\"pid\"></i>If <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">REF_EXPR</span></span> is a tuple, then <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">IDX_EXPR</span></span> must be a compile-time constant, because tuples do not support dynamic access, because each element may be a different type.<a href=\"#p_126\" class=\"pid\">126</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_127\" class=\"pid\"></i>If <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">REF_EXPR</span></span> is a mapping and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">IDX_EXPR</span></span> evaluates to an address, then this reference evaluates to a value of type <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Maybe\" title=\"rsh: Maybe\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Maybe</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">TYPE</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">)</span></span>, where <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">TYPE</span></span> is the type of the mapping.<a href=\"#p_127\" class=\"pid\">127</a></p>\n<h3 id=\"array--tuple-length--tuplelength---arraylength--and--length\" class=\"refHeader\">Array &amp; tuple length: <code>Tuple.length</code>, <code>Array.length</code>, class=\"pid\">129</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_130\" class=\"pid\"></i>Both may be abbreviated as <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">expr</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_length\" title=\"rsh: length\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">length</span></a></span> where <span class=\"refHeader\">Mapping group operations<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#mapping-group-operations\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_169\" title=\"rsh: Map.reduce\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.reduce</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(map</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> z</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> f)</span></span> returns the <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fold_(higher-order_function)\">left fold</a> of the function <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">f</span></span> over the given mapping with the initial value <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">z</span></span>.\n  For example, <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">m</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_reduce\" title=\"rsh: reduce\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.reduce</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">0</span><span style=\"color: href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_map\" title=\"rsh: map\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">map</span></a><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_reduce\" title=\"rsh: reduce\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> f)</span></span>.<a href=\"#p_170\" class=\"pid\">170</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_171\" class=\"pid\"></i>The function <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">f</span></span> must satisfy the property, for all <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">z</span></span>, <span class=\"snip\"><span var(--shiki-color-text)\">(z</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b)</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> a) </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_==\" title=\"rsh: ==\"><span style=\"color: class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">obj</span></span>,\n  except that field <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">fld</span></span> is <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">val</span></span> if <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">fld</span></span> is not already present in <span var(--shiki-token-constant)\">2</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">]);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_181\" class=\"pid\"></i>A <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_struct\">struct</span> is a combination of a tuple and an object.\n  It has named elements, like an object, but is ordered like a tuple, so its elements may be accessed by either name or position.\n  Structs exist for interfacing with non-Reach remote objects, where both parties must agree to the runtime representation of the values.<a href=\"#p_181\" class=\"pid\">181</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_182\" class=\"pid\"></i>A struct instance may be constructed by calling the <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">fromTuple</span></span> method of a struct type instance (like <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Posn</span></span>) with a tuple of the appropriate length.<a href=\"#p_182\" class=\"pid\">182</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_183\" class=\"pid\"></i>A struct instance may be constructed by calling the <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">fromObject</span></span> method of a struct type instance (like <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Posn</span></span>) with an object with the appropriate fields.<a href=\"#p_183\" class=\"pid\">183</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_184\" class=\"pid\"></i>Structs may be converted into a corresponding tuple or object via the <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">toTuple</span></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">toObject</span></span> methods on the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Struct\" title=\"rsh: Struct\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Struct</span></a></span> value (as well as struct type instances, like <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Posn</span></span> in the example above):<a href=\"#p_184\" class=\"pid\">184</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">DATA</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.VARIANT</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">VALUE</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">)</span></span>, where <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">DATA</span></span> is <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Data\" title=\"rsh: Data\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Data</span></a></span> type, <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">VARIANT</span></span> is the name of one of <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">DATA</span></span>'s variants, and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">VALUE</span></span> is a value matching the type of the variant.\n  As a special case, when the type of a variant is <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Null\" title=\"rsh: Null\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Null</span></a></span>, the <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">VALUE</span></span> may be omitted, as shown in the definition of <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">burger</span></span> in the same above.<a href=\"#p_187\" class=\"pid\">187</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_188\" class=\"pid\"></i>Data instances are consumed by <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_switch\" title=\"rsh: switch\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">switch</span></a></span> statements and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_match\" title=\"rsh: match\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">match</span></a></span> expressions.<a href=\"#p_188\" class=\"pid\">188</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_189\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_isDataVariant\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"isDataVariant\"></span>Data instances may be checked against particular variants with the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_isDataVariant\" title=\"rsh: isDataVariant\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">isDataVariant</span></a></span> function.<a href=\"#p_189\" class=\"pid\">189</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"isDataVariant(&quot;Circle&quot;, [&quot;Circle&quot;, &quot;Square&quot;, &quot;Rect&quot;], nice); // true\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn99\" title=\"Copy to title=\"rsh: Data\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Data</span></a></span> type, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Maybe\" title=\"rsh: Maybe\"><span style=\"color: title=\"rsh: Data\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Data</span></a></span> type specialized to a particular type in the <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: title=\"rsh: fromMaybe\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">fromMaybe</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(mValue</span><span style=\"color: href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Either\" title=\"rsh: Either\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Either</span></a></span> can be used to represent values with two possible types.<a href=\"#p_201\" class=\"pid\">201</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_202\" class=\"pid\"></i>Similar to <code>Maybe</code>, <code>Either</code> may be used to represent values that are correct or erroneous.\n  A successful result is stored, by convention, in <code>Right</code>. Unlike <code>None</code>, <code>Left</code> may\n  carry additional information about the error.<a href=\"#p_202\" class=\"pid\">202</a>\n</p>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_either\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"either\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"either(e, onLeft, <code>e</code>.<a href=\"#p_203\" class=\"pid\">203</a></p>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_isLeft\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"isLeft\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_isRight\" });</span></li><li value=\"14\"></li><li value=\"15\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_assert\" title=\"rsh: assert\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">assert</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">isTruthy</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(v2));</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_209\" class=\"pid\"></i>A <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_match%20expression\">match expression</span>, written <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">VAR</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_match\" title=\"rsh: match\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.match</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">({ CASE </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">...</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> })</span></span>, where <code>VAR</code> is a variable\n  bound to a data instance and <code>CASE</code> is <code>VARIANT: FUNCTION</code>, where <code>VARIANT</code> is a\n  variant or <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_default\" title=\"rsh: default\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">default</span></a></span>, and <code>FUNCTION</code> is a function that takes the same arguments as the\n  variant constructor.\n  If the variant has a type of <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Null\" title=\"rsh: Null\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Null</span></a></span>, then the function is allowed to take no arguments.\n  <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_default\" title=\"rsh: default\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">default</span></a></span> functions must always take an argument, even if all defaulted variants have type <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Null\" title=\"rsh: Null\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Null</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_209\" class=\"pid\">209</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_210\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_match\" title=\"rsh: match\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">match</span></a></span> is similar to a switch statement, but since it is an expression, it\n  can be conveniently used in places like the right hand side of an assignment statement.<a href=\"#p_210\" class=\"pid\">210</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_211\" class=\"pid\"></i>Similar to a switch statement, the cases are expected to be exhaustive and nonredundant,\n  all cases have empty tails, and it may only include a consensus transfer in\n  its cases if it is within a consensus step.<a href=\"#p_211\" class=\"pid\">211</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"conditional-expression\" class=\"refHeader\">Conditional expression<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#conditional-expression\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_?\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"?\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"choosesFirst ? [ heap1 - amount, heap2 ] : [ heap1, heap2 - amount ]\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn114\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">choosesFirst </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_?\" title=\"rsh: ?\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">?</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> [ heap1 </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_-\" title=\"rsh: -\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">-</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> amount</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> heap2 ] </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> [ heap1</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> heap2 </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_-\" title=\"rsh: -\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">-</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> amount ]</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_212\" class=\"pid\"></i>A <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_conditional%20expression\">conditional expression</span>, written <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">COND_E</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_?\" title=\"rsh: ?\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">?</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">NOT_FALSE_E</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">FALSE_E</span></span>, where <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">COND_E</span></span>, <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">NOT_FALSE_E</span></span>, and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">FALSE_E</span></span> are expressions, selects between the values which <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">NOT_FALSE_E</span></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">FALSE_E</span></span> evaluate to based on whether <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">COND_E</span></span> evaluates to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_false\" title=\"rsh: false\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">false</span></a></span>.\n  This expression will evaluate both the false and not-false sides of the\n  computation if they are considered pure.\n  Arithmetic is considered pure if you enable <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">verifyArithmetic}</span></span> or use <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">veri</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_*\" title=\"rsh: *\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">*</span></a></span> functions, like <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_safeAdd\" title=\"rsh: safeAdd\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">safeAdd</span></a></span>.\n  Arithmetic is not considered pure if you do not enable <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_verifyArithmetic\" title=\"rsh: verifyArithmetic\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">verifyArithmetic</span></a></span>, or use <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">safe</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_*\" title=\"rsh: *\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">*</span></a></span> functions, like <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_safeAdd\" title=\"rsh: safeAdd\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">safeAdd</span></a></span>, which may cause arithmetic faults.<a href=\"#p_212\" class=\"pid\">212</a>\n</p>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_ite\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"ite\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"ite(choosesFirst, [heap1 - amount, heap2], [heap1, heap2 - amount])\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn115\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_ite\" title=\"rsh: ite\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">ite</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(choosesFirst</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> [heap1 </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_-\" title=\"rsh: -\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">-</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> amount</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> heap2]</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> [heap1</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> heap2 </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_-\" title=\"rsh: -\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">-</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> amount])</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_213\" class=\"pid\"></i>Conditional expressions may also be written with the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_ite\" title=\"rsh: ite\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">ite</span></a></span> function,\n  however, note that this function always evaluates both of its branches.<a href=\"#p_213\" class=\"pid\">213</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"arrow-expression\" class=\"refHeader\">Arrow expression<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#arrow-expression\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_=%3E\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"=>\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet assert(x + y == 3); })(1, 2);\n((x, y) => { assert(x + y == 3); })(...[1, 2]);\n((x, y = 2) => { assert(x + y == 3); })(1);\n((x, y = 2) => { assert(x + y == 2); })(1, 1);\n(([x, y]) => { assert(x + y var(--shiki-color-text)\">)</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_214\" class=\"pid\"></i>An <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_arrow%20expression\">arrow expression</span>, written <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(LHS_0</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> ...</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> LHS_n) </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_=%3E\" title=\"rsh: =>\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=&gt;</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">EXPR</span></span>, where <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">LHS_0</span></span> through <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">LHS_n</span></span> are left-hand sides and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">EXPR</span></span> is an expression, evaluates to a function which is an abstraction of <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">EXPR</span></span> over <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">n</span></span> values compatible with the respective left-hand side.\n  Like function definitions, arrow expressions may use default argument notation and rest parameters.<a href=\"#p_214\" class=\"pid\">214</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"makeenum\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>makeEnum</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#makeenum\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_makeEnum\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"makeEnum\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"const [ isHand, ROCK, PAPER, SCISSORS ] = makeEnum(3);\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn117\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> [ </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">isHand</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">ROCK</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">PAPER</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">SCISSORS</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> ] </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_makeEnum\" title=\"rsh: makeEnum\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">makeEnum</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">3</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_215\" class=\"pid\"></i>An <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_enumeration\">enumeration</span> (or <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_enum\">enum</span>, for short),\n  can be created by calling the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_makeEnum\" title=\"rsh: makeEnum\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">makeEnum</span></a></span> function, as in <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_makeEnum\" title=\"rsh: makeEnum\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">makeEnum</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">N</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">)</span></span>,\n  where <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">N</span></span> is the number of distinct values in the enum.\n  This produces a tuple of <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">N</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_+\" title=\"rsh: +\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">+</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">1</span></span> values,\n  where the first value is a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Fun\" title=\"rsh: Fun\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Fun</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">([UInt]</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Bool)</span></span>\n  which tells you if its argument is one of the enum's values,\n  and the next N values are distinct <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span>s.<a href=\"#p_215\" class=\"pid\">215</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a href=\"https://github.com/reach-sh/reach-lang/tree/master/examples/secured-loan/index.rsh\">/examples/secured-loan/index.rsh</a><a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"const [ isOutcome, LENDER_TIMEOUT, BORROWER_TIMEOUT ] = makeEnum(2);\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn118\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"13\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> [ </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">isOutcome</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">LENDER_TIMEOUT</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">BORROWER_TIMEOUT</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> ] </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_makeEnum\" title=\"rsh: makeEnum\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">makeEnum</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">2</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_216\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>isOutcome</code> is a function that takes a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span> and returns <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></span> or <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_false\" title=\"rsh: false\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">false</span></a></span> depending on if the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span> passed to it is a member of that enumeration or not.\n  <code>LENDER_TIMEOUT</code> and <code>BORROWER_TIMEOUT</code> are <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span>s.<a href=\"#p_216\" class=\"pid\">216</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_217\" class=\"pid\"></i>So <code>isOutcome(LENDER_TIMEOUT)</code> would return <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></span> while <code>isOutcome(SCISSORS)</code> would return <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_false\" title=\"rsh: false\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">false</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_217\" class=\"pid\">217</a></p>\n<h3 id=\"assert\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>assert</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#assert\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_assert\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"assert\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"assert( claim, [msg] )\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn119\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_assert\" title=\"rsh: assert\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">assert</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">( claim</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> [msg] )</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p><i id=\"p_218\" href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_218\" class=\"pid\">218</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_219\" style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<div class=\"note\">\n  <p>\n    <i id=\"p_220\" class=\"pid\"></i>The Reach compiler will produce a counter-example (i.e. an assignment of the identifiers in the program to falsify the <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">claim</span></span>) when an invalid <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">claim</span></span> is provided.\n    It is possible to write a <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">claim</span></span> that actually always evaluates to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></span>, but for which our current approach cannot prove always evaluates to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></span>; if this is the case, Reach will fail to compile the program, reporting that its analysis is incomplete.\n    Reach will never produce an erroneous counter-example.<a href=\"#p_220\" class=\"pid\">220</a>\n  </p>\n</div>\n<p><i id=\"p_221\" class=\"pid\"></i>It accepts an optional bytes argument, which is included in any reported violation.<a href=\"#p_221\" class=\"pid\">221</a></p>\n<div class=\"note\">\n  <p><i id=\"p_222\" class=\"pid\"></i>See <a href=\"/guide/assert/#guide-assert\">the guide section on verification</a> to better understand how and what to verify in your program.<a href=\"#p_222\" class=\"pid\">222</a></p>\n</div>\n<h3 id=\"check\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>check</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#check\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_check\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"check\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div dynamic assertion that <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">claim</span></span> evaluates to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></span>, which expands to either a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_require\" title=\"rsh: require\"><span class=\"pid\">223</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_224\" class=\"pid\"></i>For example, <code>A</code> makes the following <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_check\" title=\"rsh: check\"><span var(--shiki-color-text)\">);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<h3 id=\"enforce\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>enforce</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#enforce\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_enforce\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"enforce\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"enforce( claim, [msg] )\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn124\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_enforce\" title=\"rsh: enforce\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">enforce</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">( claim</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> [msg] )</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_226\" class=\"pid\"></i>A dynamic assertion that <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">claim</span></span> evaluates to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></span>.\n  Since this is neither <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/local/#rsh_assume\" title=\"rsh: assume\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">assume</span></a></span> or <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_require\" title=\"rsh: require\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">require</span></a></span> it is not part of Reach's rely-guarantee reasoning analysis, thus you should avoid it as much as possible.\n  It accepts an optional bytes argument, which is included in any reported violation.<a href=\"#p_226\" class=\"pid\">226</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"forall\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>forall</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#forall\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_forall\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"forall\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"forall( Type )\nforall( Type, (var) => BLOCK )\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn125\" title=\"Copy to class=\"pid\"></i>The single argument version returns an abstract value of the given type.\n  It may only be referenced inside of assertions; any other reference is invalid.<a href=\"#p_227\" class=\"pid\">227</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_228\" class=\"pid\"></i>The two argument version is an abbreviation of calling the second argument with the result of <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_forall\" title=\"rsh: forall\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">forall</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(Type)</span></span>.\n  This is convenient for writing general claims about expressions, such as<a href=\"#p_228\" class=\"pid\">228</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far id=\"p_246\" class=\"pid\"></i>The <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_thisConsensusTime\">thisConsensusTime</span> primitive returns the network time of the current publication of the DApp.<a href=\"#p_246\" class=\"pid\">246</a></p>\n<div class=\"note\">\n  <p><i id=\"p_247\" class=\"pid\"></i>Some networks do not support observing the time of a consensus operation until after it has finalized.<a href=\"#p_247\" class=\"pid\">247</a></p>\n</div>\n<hr>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_thisConsensusSecs\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"thisConsensusSecs\"></span></p>\n<pre var(--shiki-token-function)\">thisConsensusSecs</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">()</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p><i id=\"p_248\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"term\" set <code>lastTime</code> to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_thisConsensusTime\" title=\"rsh: thisConsensusTime\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">thisConsensusTime</span></a></span>, <code>lastSecs</code> to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_thisConsensusSecs\" title=\"rsh: thisConsensusSecs\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">thisConsensusSecs</span></a></span> and <code>i</code> to 0.\n  Then, an invariant is set to make sure that <code>lastTime</code> is greater than <span <code>lastTime</code> is equal to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_thisConsensusTime\" title=\"rsh: thisConsensusTime\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">thisConsensusTime</span></a></span>, <code>lastSecs</code> is either equal or greater than <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_lastConsensusSecs\" title=\"rsh: lastConsensusSecs\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">lastConsensusSecs</span></a></span> and that the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_balance\" title=\"rsh: balance\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">balance</span></a></span> is equal to 0.\n  This makes sure that the order of blocks matches the order of time.<a href=\"#p_249\" class=\"pid\">249</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"basewaittime--and--basewaitsecs\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>baseWaitTime</code> and <code>baseWaitSecs</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" It then sets <code>lastTime</code> to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_thisConsensusTime\" title=\"rsh: thisConsensusTime\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">thisConsensusTime</span></a></span>, <code>lastSecs</code> to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_baseWaitSecs\" title=\"rsh: baseWaitSecs\"><span style=\"color: <code>lastSecs</code> is either equal or greater than <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_baseWaitSecs\" title=\"rsh: baseWaitSecs\"><span style=\"color: id=\"time-arguments----relativetime---absolutetime---relativesecs---absolutesecs\" class=\"refHeader\">Time arguments - <code>relativeTime</code>, <code>absoluteTime</code>, <code>relativeSecs</code>, <code>absoluteSecs</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#time-arguments----relativetime---absolutetime---relativesecs---absolutesecs\"><span class=\"icon var(--shiki-color-text)\">claim)</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p><i id=\"p_252\" class=\"pid\"></i>These functions return <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_time%20arguments\">time arguments</span>, which are instances of the type <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Either\" title=\"rsh: Either\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Either</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(UInt</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> UInt)</span></span>, where <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Left</span></span> variants refer to absolute network time and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Right</span></span> variants refer to absolute network seconds.<a href=\"#p_252\" class=\"pid\">252</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_253\" class=\"pid\"></i>These functions take an optional function argument, <code>claim</code>, which will be used to verify arithmetic when necessary.\n  In most cases, one would pass <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_check\" title=\"rsh: check\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">check</span></a></span> or <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_assert\" title=\"rsh: assert\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">assert</span></a></span>.\n  This argument is only needed when <code>verifyArithmetic</code> is enabled.\n  The default value of this argument is a no-op.<a href=\"#p_253\" class=\"pid\">253</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_254\" class=\"pid\"></i>The <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_absoluteTime\" title=\"rsh: absoluteTime\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">absoluteTime</span></a></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_absoluteSecs\" title=\"rsh: absoluteSecs\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">absoluteSecs</span></a></span> are equivalent to <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Left</span></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Right</span></span> variant tags, respectively.<a href=\"#p_254\" class=\"pid\">254</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_255\" class=\"pid\"></i>Example:<a href=\"#p_255\" class=\"pid\">255</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a })\n        .timeout(absoluteTime(end), () => {\n            Creator.publish();\n            return [highestBidder, lastPrice, isFirstBid];\n        });\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn150\" title=\"Copy to class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_makeDeadline\" title=\"rsh: makeDeadline\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">makeDeadline</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(deadline)</span></span> takes a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span> as an argument and returns a pair of functions\n  that can be used for dealing with absolute deadlines. It internally determines the end time based off of the deadline\n  and the last consensus time—at the time of calling <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_makeDeadline\" title=\"rsh: makeDeadline\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">makeDeadline</span></a></span>. <code>timeRemaining</code> will calculate the difference\n  between the end time and the current last consensus time. <code>keepGoing</code> determines whether the current last consensus time\n  is less than the end time. It is typical to use the two fields for the <code>while</code> and <code>timeout</code> field of a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_parallelReduce\" title=\"rsh: parallelReduce\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">parallelReduce</span></a></span>\n  expression. backend on line 6.<a href=\"#p_273\" class=\"pid\">273</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"compose\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>compose</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#compose\"><span class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"compose(f, g)\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn167\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_compose\" title=\"rsh: compose\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">compose</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(f</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> g)</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_274\" class=\"pid\"></i>Creates a new function that applies its argument to <code>g</code>, then pipes the result to the function <code>f</code>.\n  The argument type of <code>f</code> must be the return type of <code>g</code>.<a href=\"#p_274\" class=\"pid\">274</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"muldiv\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>muldiv</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#muldiv\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<div class=\"note\">\n  <p><i id=\"p_275\" class=\"pid\"></i>Currently, wide arithmetic operations are only suported on Algorand.<a href=\"#p_275\" class=\"pid\">275</a></p>\n</div>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_muldiv\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"muldiv\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"muldiv(a, b, c)\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn168\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_muldiv\" title=\"rsh: muldiv\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">muldiv</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(a</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> b</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> c)</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_276\" class=\"pid\"></i>Multiplies <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">a</span></span> by <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">b</span></span>, then immediately divides the product by <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">c</span></span>.\n  The intermediate value may be larger than <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">UInt</span></a><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt.max\" title=\"rsh: UInt.max\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.max</span></a></span> if the connector supports wide arithmetic operations.\n  The resulting quotient must be less than <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">UInt</span></a><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt.max\" title=\"rsh: UInt.max\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.max</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_276\" class=\"pid\">276</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a href=\"https://github.com/reach-sh/reach-lang/tree/master/examples/pr855/index.rsh\">/examples/pr855/index.rsh</a><a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"        if (curTime < start) The output would then be divided by <code>duration</code> immediately.<a href=\"#p_277\" class=\"pid\">277</a></p>\n<h3 id=\"verimuldiv\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>veriMuldiv</code><a generates a claim that the result of applying the same arguments to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_muldiv\" title=\"rsh: muldiv\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">muldiv</span></a></span> will not overflow.\n  When used inside of a local step or export, it will generate an <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/local/#rsh_assume\" <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_assert\" title=\"rsh: assert\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">assert</span></a></span> claim.<a href=\"#p_281\" muldiv\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">muldiv</span></a></span> is used on line 36 to multiply <code>x</code> and <code>y</code>.\n  After which, the product of <code>x</code> and <code>y</code> is immediately divided by the product of <code>cx</code> and <code>cy</code>.\n  On line 41, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_verifyMuldiv\" title=\"rsh: verifyMuldiv\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">verifyMuldiv</span></a></span> is used with the same arguments passed to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_muldiv\" title=\"rsh: muldiv\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">muldiv</span></a></span> on line 36.\n  In this case, however, it is used to generate a claim that the result of applying the same arguments to\n  <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_muldiv\" title=\"rsh: muldiv\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">muldiv</span></a></span> will not overflow.<a href=\"#p_282\" class=\"pid\">282</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"sqrt\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>sqrt</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#sqrt\"><span class=\"icon
