href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_sqrt\" title=\"rsh: sqrt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">sqrt</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">81</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">)</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p><i id=\"p_283\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_sqrt\" title=\"rsh: sqrt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">sqrt</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(x)</span></span> returns the largest integer <code>i</code> such that <code>i * i &lt;= x</code>.<a href=\"#p_283\" class=\"pid\">283</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a href=\"https://github.com/reach-sh/reach-lang/tree/master/examples/sqrt/index.rsh\">/examples/sqrt/index.rsh</a><a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"    A.publish(x, z);\n    check(z == sqrt(x));\n    commit();\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn175\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"17\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">    </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">A</span><a href=\"/rsh/step/#rsh_publish\" title=\"rsh: publish\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.publish</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(x</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> z);</span></li><li value=\"18\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">    </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_check\" title=\"rsh: check\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">check</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(z </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_==\" title=\"rsh: ==\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">==</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_sqrt\" title=\"rsh: sqrt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">sqrt</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(x));</span></li><li value=\"19\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">    </span><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_commit\" title=\"rsh: commit\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">commit</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">();</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_284\" class=\"pid\"></i>This code checks if <code>z</code> is equivalent to the square root of <code>x</code> on line 18.\n  For example, if <code>z</code> is 9 and <code>x</code> is 81, that line would return <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_284\" class=\"pid\">284</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"sqrtapprox\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>sqrtApprox</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#sqrtapprox\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_sqrtApprox\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"sqrtApprox\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"sqrtApprox(81, 10)\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn176\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_sqrtApprox\" title=\"rsh: sqrtApprox\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">sqrtApprox</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">81</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">10</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">)</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_285\" class=\"pid\"></i>Calculates an approximate square root of the first argument.\n  This method utilizes the <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Methods_of_computing_square_roots#Babylonian_method\">Babylonian Method</a> for computing the square root.\n  The second argument must be a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span> whose value is known at compile time, which represents the number of iterations the algorithm should perform.<a href=\"#p_285\" class=\"pid\">285</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_286\" class=\"pid\"></i>For reference, when performing <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">5</span></span> iterations, the algorithm can reliably calculate the square root up to <code>32</code> squared, or <code>1,024</code>.\n  When performing <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">10</span></span> iterations, the algorithm can reliably calculate the square root up to <code>580</code> squared, or <code>336,400</code>.<a href=\"#p_286\" class=\"pid\">286</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"pow\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>pow</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#pow\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_pow\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"pow\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"pow (2, 40, 10) // => 1,099,511,627,776\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn177\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_pow\" title=\"rsh: pow\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">pow</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> (</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">2</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">10</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">) </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// =&gt; 1,099,511,627,776</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_287\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_pow\" title=\"rsh: pow\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">pow</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(base</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> power</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> precision)</span></span> calculates the approximate value of raising base to power.\n  The third argument must be a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span> whose value is known at compile time, which represents the number\n  of iterations the algorithm should perform.<a href=\"#p_287\" class=\"pid\">287</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_288\" class=\"pid\"></i>Example:<a href=\"#p_288\" class=\"pid\">288</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a 3;\n  const finalOutcome = pow(outcome, handAlice + handBob, 10);\n  commit();\n\n  each([Alice, Bob], () => {\n    interact.seeOutcome(finalOutcome);\n  });\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn178\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"28\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">  </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span title=\"rsh: +\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">+</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> (</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">4</span><span var(--shiki-token-function)\">.seeOutcome</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(finalOutcome);</span></li><li value=\"34\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">  });</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_289\" class=\"pid\"></i>This code computes the <code>finalOutcome</code> of the <code>Rock, Paper, Scissors</code> game using the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_pow\" title=\"rsh: pow\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">pow</span></a></span> method.\n  It takes <code>outcome</code> as the <code>base</code>, the sum of <code>handAlice</code> and <code>handBob</code> as the <code>power</code>, and <code>10</code> as the <code>precision</code>.<a href=\"#p_289\" class=\"pid\">289</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_290\" class=\"pid\"></i>For reference, <code>6</code> iterations provides enough accuracy to calculate up to <code>2^64 - 1</code>, so the largest power it can compute is <code>2^63</code>.\n  If the number of iterations is not large enough to compute the power, then the result is completely inaccurate.\n  It is recommended to create <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_assert\" title=\"rsh: assert\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">assert</span></a></span> tests to ensure the possible values your program can compute are accurate.<a href=\"#p_290\" class=\"pid\">290</a>\n</p>\n<h3 id=\"signed-integers\" class=\"refHeader\">Signed Integers<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#signed-integers\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_291\" class=\"pid\"></i>The standard library provides abstractions for dealing with signed integers. The following definitions\n  are used to represent <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Int\" title=\"rsh: Int\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Int</span></a></span>s:<a href=\"#p_291\" class=\"pid\">291</a>\n</p>\n<div class=\"note\">\n  <p>\n    <i id=\"p_292\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>Int</code> is represented as an object, as opposed to a scalar value, because some platforms\n    that Reach targets do not provide native support for signed integers.<a href=\"#p_292\" class=\"pid\">292</a>\n  </p>\n</div>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Int\" data-scope=\"rsh\" var(--shiki-color-text)\">;</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_293\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_int\" title=\"rsh: int\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">int</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(Bool</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_isub\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"isub\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_isub\" title=\"rsh: isub\"><span style=\"color: <code>y</code> from the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Int\" title=\"rsh: Int\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Int</span></a></span> <code>x</code>.<a href=\"#p_295\" style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Int</span></a></span> <code>x</code> and the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Int\" title=\"rsh: Int\"><span style=\"color: href=\"#p_302\" class=\"pid\">302</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_303\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_ieq\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"ieq\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a class=\"pid\">303</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_304\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_ine\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"ine\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_ine\" class=\"pid\">304</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_305\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_imax\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"imax\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a Int\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Int</span></a></span>s.<a href=\"#p_305\" class=\"pid\">305</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_306\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_abs\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"abs\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_abs\" title=\"rsh: abs\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">abs</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(i)</span></span> returns the absolute value of an <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Int\" title=\"rsh: Int\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Int</span></a></span>. The return value is of type <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_306\" class=\"pid\">306</a></p>\n<h3 id=\"fixed-point-numbers\" class=\"refHeader\">Fixed-Point Numbers<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#fixed-point-numbers\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><i id=\"p_307\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_FixedPoint\" title=\"rsh: FixedPoint\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">FixedPoint</span></a></span> is defined by<a href=\"#p_307\" class=\"pid\">307</a></p>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_FixedPoint\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"FixedPoint\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"export const FixedPoint = Object({ sign: bool, i: Object({ scale: UInt, i: UInt }) });\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn181\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/module/#rsh_export\" title=\"rsh: export\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">export</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_FixedPoint\" title=\"rsh: FixedPoint\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">FixedPoint</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Object\" title=\"rsh: Object\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Object</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">({ sign</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> bool</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> i</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Object\" title=\"rsh: Object\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Object</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">({ scale</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> UInt</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> i</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> UInt }) });</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_308\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_FixedPoint\" title=\"rsh: FixedPoint\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">FixedPoint</span></a></span> can be used to represent numbers with a fixed number of digits after the decimal point.\n  They are handy for representing fractional values, especially in base 10. The value of a fixed point number is determined\n  by dividing the underlying integer value, <code>i</code>, by its scale factor, <code>scale</code>. For example, we could\n  represent the value <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">1.234</span></span> with <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">{ sign</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Pos</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> i</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> { scale</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">1000</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> i </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">1234</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> } }</span></span> or <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_fx\" title=\"rsh: fx\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">fx</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">1000</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">)(Pos</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">1234</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">)</span></span>.\n  Alternatively, Reach provides syntactic sugar for defining <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_FixedPoint\" title=\"rsh: FixedPoint\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">FixedPoint</span></a></span> numbers. One can simply write\n  <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">1.234</span></span>, which will assume the value is in base 10. A scale factor of <code>1000</code> correlates to 3 decimal\n  places of precision. Similarly, a scale factor of <code>100</code> would have 2 decimal places of precision.<a href=\"#p_308\" class=\"pid\">308</a>\n</p>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_fx\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"fx\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"const scale = 10;\nconst i = 56;\nfx(scale)(Neg, i); // represents - 5.6\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn182\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">scale</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">10</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">;</span></li><li value=\"2\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">i</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">56</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">;</span></li><li value=\"3\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_fx\" title=\"rsh: fx\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">fx</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(scale)(Neg</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> i); </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// represents - 5.6</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_309\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_fx\" title=\"rsh: fx\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">fx</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(scale)(i)</span></span> will return a function that can be used to\n  instantiate fixed point numbers with a particular scale factor.<a href=\"#p_309\" class=\"pid\">309</a>\n</p>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_fxint\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"fxint\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"const i = 4;\nfxint(-i); // represents - 4.0\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn183\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">i</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">4</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">;</span></li><li value=\"2\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_fxint\" title=\"rsh: fxint\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">fxint</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_-\" title=\"rsh: -\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">-</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">i); </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// represents - 4.0</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_310\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_fxint\" title=\"rsh: fxint\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">fxint</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(Int)</span></span> will cast the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Int\" title=\"rsh: Int\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Int</span></a></span> arg as a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_FixedPoint\" title=\"rsh: FixedPoint\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">FixedPoint</span></a></span>\n  number with a <code>scale</code> of 1.<a href=\"#p_310\" class=\"pid\">310</a>\n</p>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_fxrescale\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"fxrescale\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"const x = fx(1000)(Pos, 1234); // x = 1.234\nfxrescale(x, 100);    // => 1.23\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn184\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">x</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_fx\" title=\"rsh: fx\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">fx</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">1000</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">)(Pos</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">1234</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">); </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// x = 1.234</span></li><li value=\"2\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_fxrescale\" title=\"rsh: fxrescale\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">fxrescale</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(x</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">100</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">);    </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// =&gt; 1.23</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_311\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_fxrescale\" title=\"rsh: fxrescale\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">fxrescale</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(x</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> scale)</span></span> will convert a fixed point number from using\n  one scale to another. This operation can result in loss of precision, as demonstrated in the above example.<a href=\"#p_311\" class=\"pid\">311</a>\n</p>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_fxunify\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"fxunify\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"const x = fx(1000)(Pos, 824345); // x = 824.345\nconst y = 45.67;\nfxunify(x, y);    // => [ 1000, 824.345, 45.670 ]\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn185\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">x</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_fx\" title=\"rsh: fx\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">fx</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">1000</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">)(Pos</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">824345</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">); </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// x = 824.345</span></li><li value=\"2\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">y</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">45.67</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">;</span></li><li value=\"3\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_fxunify\" title=\"rsh: fxunify\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">fxunify</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(x</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> y);    </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// =&gt; [ 1000, 824.345, 45.670 ]</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_312\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_fxunify\" title=\"rsh: fxunify\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">fxunify</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(x</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> y)</span></span> will convert the fixed point numbers\n  to use the same scale. The larger scale of the two arguments will be chosen. The function will return a <code>3-tuple</code> consisting\n  of the common scale and the newly scaled values.<a href=\"#p_312\" class=\"pid\">312</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_313\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_fxadd\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"fxadd\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_fxadd\" title=\"rsh: fxadd\"><span style=\"color: fxpow(base, power, 10, 1000000); // 1.259921</span></span><a href=\"#p_321\" class=\"pid\">321</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_322\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_fxpow\" title=\"rsh: fxpow\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">fxpow</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(base</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> power</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> precision</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> scalePrecision)</span></span> approximates the power of the fixed number, <code>base</code>,\n  raised to the fixed point number, <code>power</code>. The third argument must be a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span> whose value is known\n  at compile time, which represents the number of iterations the algorithm should perform.\n  The <code>scalePrecision</code> argument must be a <code>UInt</code> and represents the scale of the return value. Choosing a larger\n  <code>scalePrecision</code> allows for more precision when approximating the power, as demonstrated in the example below:<a href=\"#p_322\" class=\"pid\">322</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_323\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_fxpowi\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"fxpowi\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_fxpowi\" title=\"rsh: fxpowi\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">fxpowi</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(base</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> power</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> precision)</span></span> approximates the power of the fixed number, <code>base</code>,\n  raised to the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Int\" title=\"rsh: Int\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Int</span></a></span>, <code>power</code>. The third argument must be a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span> whose value is known\n  at compile time, which represents the number of iterations the algorithm should perform. For reference, <code>6</code> iterations\n  provides enough accuracy to calculate up to <code>2^64 - 1</code>, so the largest power it can compute is <code>63</code>.<a href=\"#p_323\" class=\"pid\">323</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_324\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_fxpowui\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"fxpowui\"></span><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_fxpowui\" title=\"rsh: fxpowui\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">fxpowui</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">5.8</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">3</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">10</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">); </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// 195.112</span></span><a href=\"#p_324\" class=\"pid\">324</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_325\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_fxpowui\" title=\"rsh: fxpowui\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">fxpowui</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(base</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> power</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> precision)</span></span> approximates the power of\n  the fixed number, <code>base</code>, raised to the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span>, <code>power</code>. The third\n  argument must be a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span> whose value is known at compile time.<a href=\"#p_325\" class=\"pid\">325</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_326\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_fxcmp\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"fxcmp\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_Anybody\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"Anybody\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" race(...Participants).publish()</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_334\" class=\"pid\"></i>Reach provides a shorthand, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Anybody\" title=\"rsh: Anybody\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Anybody</span></a></span>, which serves as a\n  <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/step/#rsh_race\" title=\"rsh: race\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">race</span></a></span> between all participants.\n  This shorthand can be useful for situations where\n  it does not matter who <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/step/#rsh_publish\" title=\"rsh: publish\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">publish</span></a></span>es, such as in a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/step/#rsh_timeout\" title=\"rsh: timeout\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">timeout</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_334\" class=\"pid\">334</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_335\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Anybody\" title=\"rsh: Anybody\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Anybody</span></a></span> is strictly an abbreviation of a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/step/#rsh_race\" title=\"rsh: race\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">race</span></a></span> involving all of the named participants of the application.<a class=\"codeHeader\"><a href=\"https://github.com/reach-sh/reach-lang/tree/master/examples/multiple-pr-case/index.rsh\">/examples/multiple-pr-case/index.rsh</a><a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" with a participant class, this means any principal at all, because there is no restriction on which principals (i.e. addresses) may serve as a member of that class.\n  In an application without any participant classes, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Anybody\" title=\"rsh: Anybody\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Anybody</span></a></span> instead would mean only <code>i</code>.<a href=\"#p_403\" class=\"pid\">403</a></p>\n<h3 id=\"getuntrackedfunds\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>getUntrackedFunds</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"const f1 = getUntrackedFunds();\ntransfer(f1).to(Alice);\nconst f2 = getUntrackedFunds(tok);\ntransfer(f2, tok).to(Alice);\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn217\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.to</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(Alice);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_404\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_getUntrackedFunds\" title=\"rsh: getUntrackedFunds\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">getUntrackedFunds</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_?\" title=\"rsh: ?\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">?</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">token)</span></span> takes an optional <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Token\" title=\"rsh: Token\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Token</span></a></span> argument and returns the difference between the actual balance of the contract and Reach's expectation of the balance for the given token, or network token if no argument is provided.\n  For example, if funds were externally sent to the contract or rewards were earned, this function gives you access to them.\n  Once this function is called, the amount returned is incorporated into Reach's expectation of the balance.\n  So, the amount returned must eventually be transferred out of the contract to satisfy the token linearity property.<a href=\"#p_404\" class=\"pid\">404</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_405\" class=\"pid\"></i>If a contract were to have its funds improperly removed, through clawback or other means, and the actual balance is less\n  than Reach's expectation, this function will return <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">0</span></span>.<a href=\"#p_405\" class=\"pid\">405</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_406\" class=\"pid\"></i>Example:<a href=\"#p_406\" class=\"pid\">406</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a href=\"https://github.com/reach-sh/reach-lang/tree/master/examples/getUntrackedFunds3/index.rsh\">/examples/getUntrackedFunds3/index.rsh</a><a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\" <code>x</code> and then transferred to <code>B</code>.<a href=\"#p_407\" class=\"pid\">407</a></p>\n<h3 id=\"distinct\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>distinct</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" id=\"currentmode\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>currentMode</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#currentmode\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_currentMode\" title=\"rsh: currentMode\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">currentMode</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">()</span></span> evaluates to a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Data\" title=\"rsh: Data\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Data</span></a></span> instance with variants <code>Module</code>, <code>AppInit</code>, <code>Step</code>, <code>Local</code>, <code>Consensus</code>, and <code>Export</code>, corresponding to the current mode of the Reach application.<a href=\"#p_411\" class=\"pid\">411</a></p>\n<h3 id=\"mixin\" class=\"refHeader\"><code>mixin</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#mixin\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"rsh_mixin\" data-scope=\"rsh\" data-symbol=\"mixin\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"const makeMixed = mixin({ Base: ..., IDs: ..., View: ..., Events: ..., API: ... });\n\nconst mixedCtc = makeMixed();\n// or, to override `Base` in the definition with above with otherMakeMixed:\nconst mixedCtc = makeMixed(otherMakeMixed);\n\n// mixed fields\nmixedCtc.IDs\nmixedCtc.View\nmixedCtc.Events\nmixedCtc.API\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn222\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">makeMixed</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_mixin\" title=\"rsh: mixin\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">mixin</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">({ Base</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">...</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> IDs</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">...</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> View</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">...</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Events</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">...</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> API</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">...</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> });</span></li><li value=\"2\"></li><li value=\"3\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">mixedCtc</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">makeMixed</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">();</span></li><li value=\"4\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// or, to override `Base` in the definition with above with otherMakeMixed:</span></li><li value=\"5\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" title=\"rsh: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">mixedCtc</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">makeMixed</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(otherMakeMixed);</span></li><li value=\"6\"></li><li value=\"7\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// mixed fields</span></li><li value=\"8\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">mixedCtc</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.IDs</span></li><li value=\"9\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">mixedCtc</span><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_View\" title=\"rsh: View\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.View</span></a></li><li value=\"10\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">mixedCtc</span><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_Events\" title=\"rsh: Events\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.Events</span></a></li><li value=\"11\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">mixedCtc</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.</span><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_API\" title=\"rsh: API\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">API</span></a></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_412\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>mixin</code> is an implementation of mixins (see <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mixin\">Wikipedia</a> or the <a href=\"https://docs.racket-lang.org/guide/classes.html#%28part._.Mixins%29\">Racket Documentation</a> for an explanation of mixins) for composing contract interfaces.\n  (These mixins are <em>only</em> for the interface, not the implementation.)<a href=\"#p_412\" class=\"pid\">412</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_413\" class=\"pid\"></i>The function takes an object that optionally contains the fields <code>IDs</code>, <code>View</code>, <code>Events</code>, and <code>API</code>.\n  This object represents the interface of a contract, where <code>IDs</code> is a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Tuple\" title=\"rsh: Tuple\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Tuple</span></a></span> of constants, <code>View</code> is a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Tuple\" title=\"rsh: Tuple\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Tuple</span></a></span> of arguments to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_View\" title=\"rsh: View\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">View</span></a></span>, <code>Events</code> is a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Tuple\" title=\"rsh: Tuple\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Tuple</span></a></span> of arguments to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_Events\" title=\"rsh: Events\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Events</span></a></span>, and <code>API</code> is a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Tuple\" title=\"rsh: Tuple\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Tuple</span></a></span> of arguments to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_API\" title=\"rsh: API\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">API</span></a></span>.\n  The object optionally also contains a <code>Base</code> field, which will be used as a default base interface when constructing the combined contract interface.<a href=\"#p_413\" class=\"pid\">413</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_414\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_mixin\" title=\"rsh: mixin\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">mixin</span></a></span> returns a function, which, when called, combines all of the base interfaces and constructs the final <code>API</code>, <code>View</code>, and <code>Events</code> (using the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_API\" title=\"rsh: API\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">API</span></a></span>, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_View\" title=\"rsh: View\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">View</span></a></span>, and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_Events\" title=\"rsh: Events\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Events</span></a></span> constructors respectively).\n  The returned function also takes an optional <code>Base</code> parameter, which will be used instead of the base interface found in the <code>Base</code> field passed to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_mixin\" title=\"rsh: mixin\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">mixin</span></a></span>.\n  (It is useful to modify the <code>Base</code> to implement a specific order of instantiation to implement multiple inheritance.)<a href=\"#p_414\" class=\"pid\">414</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_415\" class=\"pid\"></i>After composition, the individual components can be access normally.\n  For example, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_mixin\" title=\"rsh: mixin\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">mixin</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">...</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.)().</span><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_View\" title=\"rsh: View\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">View</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">v</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_set\" title=\"rsh: set\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.set</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(vv)</span></span> would set the <code>v</code> <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_View\" title=\"rsh: View\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">View</span></a></span> regardless of where the interface was defined.\n  The <code>IDs</code> component is intended to hold byte strings that represent ERC-165 interface identifiers.<a href=\"#p_415\" class=\"pid\">415</a>\n</p>\n<hr>\n<p><i id=\"p_416\" class=\"pid\"></i>For example, we define all of the interfaces that are part of the <a href=\"https://eips.ethereum.org/EIPS/eip-721\">ERC-721</a> NFT specification using <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_mixin\" title=\"rsh: mixin\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">mixin</span></a></span>:<a href=\"#p_416\" class=\"pid\">416</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a href=\"https://github.com/reach-sh/reach-lang/tree/master/examples/ERC721/index.rsh\">/examples/ERC721/index.rsh</a><a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"const ERC165 = mixin({\n  IDs: [ Bytes.fromHex('0x01ffc9a7'), ],\n  View: [{\n    supportsInterface: Fun([Bytes(4)], Bool),\n  }],\n});\n\nconst ERC721 = mixin({\n  Base: ERC165,\n  IDs: [ Bytes.fromHex('0x80ac58cd'), ],\n  View: [{\n    balanceOf: Fun([Address], UInt),\n    ownerOf: Fun([UInt], Address),\n    getApproved: Fun([UInt], Address),\n    isApprovedForAll: Fun([Address, Address], Bool),\n  }],\n  Events: [{\n    Transfer: [Address, Address, UInt],\n    Approval: [Address, Address, UInt],\n    ApprovalForAll: [Address, Address, Bool],\n  }],\n  API: [{\n    safeTransferFrom1: Fun([Address, Address, UInt, BytesDyn], Null),\n    safeTransferFrom2: Fun([Address, Address, UInt], Null),\n    transferFrom: Fun([Address, Address, UInt], Null),\n    approve: Fun([Address, UInt], Null),\n    setApprovalForAll: Fun([Address, Bool], Null),\n  }, {\n    safeTransferFrom1: 'safeTransferFrom',\n    safeTransferFrom2: 'safeTransferFrom',\n  }],\n});\n\nconst ERC721Metadata = mixin({\n  Base: ERC721,\n  IDs: [ Bytes.fromHex('0x5b5e139f'), ],\n  View: [{\n    name: StringDyn,\n    symbol: StringDyn,\n    tokenURI: Fun([UInt], StringDyn),\n  }],\n});\n\nconst ERC721Enumerable = mixin({\n  Base: ERC721,\n  IDs: [ Bytes.fromHex('0x780e9d63'), ],\n  View: [{\n    totalSupply: UInt,\n    tokenByIndex: Fun([UInt], UInt),\n    tokenOfOwnerByIndex: Fun([Address, UInt], UInt),\n  }],\n});\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn223\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"8\"><a
